<TEXT>
<!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd">

	<body style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">
<div><a name="s1003BFBC5A7924953F4ED1DE777AE6CD"></a></div><div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:right;font-size:12pt;"><img src="a8kjanuary52015image1.jpg" alt="a8kjanuary52015image1.jpg" style="height:96px;width:624px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:right;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:13pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13pt;font-weight:bold;">McCormick Appoints Gary Rodkin to Board of Directors</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">SPARKS, Md., January 24, 2017 - McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), a global leader in flavor, today announced that Gary Rodkin, retired  Chief Executive Officer (CEO) of ConAgra Foods, has been appointed to the Board of Directors of McCormick effective January 24, 2017.</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Mr. Rodkin served for 10 years at ConAgra Foods as CEO in his last executive role.  His leadership transformed ConAgra from a holding company into a unified business with a balanced portfolio of consumer, commercial and private-brand businesses, and strong operating capabilities.  During Mr. Rodkin&#8217;s tenure, there were major changes to ConAgra&#8217;s portfolio including the acquisition of Bertolli and PF Changs frozen meals, Marie Callender&#8217;s frozen pies, Ralcorp Holdings, and the joint venture formation of North America&#8217;s largest flour milling company, Ardent Mills.  Mr. Rodkin drove process reengineering and rationalization yielding significant and sustainable cost savings over his tenure.  He ramped up product innovation including the introduction of the grocery industry&#8217;s largest new product launch in 2008, Healthy Choice Caf&#233; Steamers.  Mr. Rodkin&#8217;s advocacy of talent management and operating principles improved the culture and employee engagement at ConAgra Foods. </font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Prior to joining ConAgra, Mr. Rodkin held several leadership positions at PepsiCo including Chairman and CEO of PepsiCo Beverages and Foods North America, and President and CEO of Tropicana.  Prior to PepsiCo, Mr. Rodkin spent 16 years at General Mills where he held a variety of management roles, including President of the Yoplait Yogurt division.  </font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Lawrence Kurzius, President and CEO of McCormick commented, &#8220;Mr. Rodkin brings a tremendous track record of building and acquiring strong businesses to our Board of Directors.  His wealth of experience delivering top line and bottom line growth in the beverage and consumer goods space will be a tremendous asset to McCormick as we look to deliver against our long term growth objectives.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Mr. Rodkin received a Bachelor of Arts degree in Economics from Rutgers University in 1974 and a Master of Business Administration from Harvard Business School in 1979.  He currently serves on the boards of Simon Property Group, Inc., Feeding America, and is Vice Chairman of the Rutgers University Board of Overseers.  Mr. Rodkin is also a Fellow of Executive Education at the Harvard Business School, and an Executive in Residence at Rutgers University.     </font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;font-weight:bold;">About McCormick </font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">McCormick&#160;&amp; Company, Incorporated is a global leader in flavor. With $4.3 billion in annual sales, the company manufactures, markets and distributes spices, seasoning mixes, condiments and other flavorful products to the entire food industry &#8211; retail outlets, food manufacturers and foodservice businesses.  Every day, no matter where or what you eat, you can enjoy food flavored by McCormick.  </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;font-style:italic;">McCormick Brings Passion to Flavor&#8482;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;background-color:#ffffff;">For more information, visit www.mccormickcorporation.com.</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:138%;text-align:center;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;background-color:#ffffff;">###</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;padding-bottom:13px;padding-top:18px;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;font-weight:bold;">For information contact:</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Corporate Communications:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:138%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11.5pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;">Lori Robinson (410)&#160;527-6004 or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11.5pt;text-decoration:underline;">lori_robinson@mccormick.com</font></div><div><br></div><div></div>	</body>
